Sexuality

Is this a normal sensation? How often does your finger throb up with each heartbeat?

Me
(30-35)

I cut the skin on my thumb today and now it is wrapped with a bandaid. It keeps on throbbing though, is this because the bandaid is too tight?

It's hard to explain but the closest illustration I can find is this:

It's a normal sensation
You masturbate too much
